                <div class="td-module-thumb"><a href="https://www.njartscouncil.org/painting/painters/the-human-condition-by-rene-magritte-1933-national-gallery-of-art-washington-dc-usa/" rel="bookmark" title="&#8220;The Human Condition&#8221; by René Magritte (1933, National Gallery of Art, Washington, DC, USA)"><img width="324" height="235" class="entry-thumb" src="https://www.njartscouncil.org/wp-content/uploads/2017/09/The-human-condition-magritte-324x235.jpg" srcset="https://www.njartscouncil.org/wp-content/uploads/2017/09/The-human-condition-magritte-324x235.jpg 324w, https://www.njartscouncil.org/wp-content/uploads/2017/09/The-human-condition-magritte-796x580.jpg 796w" sizes="(max-width: 324px) 100vw, 324px" alt="" title="&#8220;The Human Condition&#8221; by René Magritte (1933, National Gallery of Art, Washington, DC, USA)"/></a></div>                <a href="https://www.njartscouncil.org/painting/painters/" class="td-post-category">Painters</a>            </div>

            <h3 class="entry-title td-module-title"><a href="https://www.njartscouncil.org/painting/painters/the-human-condition-by-rene-magritte-1933-national-gallery-of-art-washington-dc-usa/" rel="bookmark" title="&#8220;The Human Condition&#8221; by René Magritte (1933, National Gallery of Art, Washington, DC, USA)">&#8220;The Human Condition&#8221; by René Magritte (1933, National Gallery of Art,...</a></h3>
            <div class="td-module-meta-info">
                <span class="td-post-author-name"><a href="https://www.njartscouncil.org/author/admin/">Eric Schöller</a> <span>-</span> </span>                <span class="td-post-date"><time class="entry-date updated td-module-date" datetime="2017-09-10T19:52:07+00:00" >September 10, 2017</time></span>                <div class="td-module-comments"><a href="https://www.njartscouncil.org/painting/painters/the-human-condition-by-rene-magritte-1933-national-gallery-of-art-washington-dc-usa/#respond">0</a></div>            </div>

            <div class="td-excerpt">

A...            </div>

                <div class="td-module-thumb"><a href="https://www.njartscouncil.org/featured/samurai-of-the-satsuma-clan-by-felice-beato/" rel="bookmark" title="&#8220;Samurai of the Satsuma Clan&#8221; by Felice Beato"><img width="324" height="235" class="entry-thumb" src="https://www.njartscouncil.org/wp-content/uploads/2017/09/Satsuma-samurai-during-boshin-war-period-324x235.jpg" alt="" title="&#8220;Samurai of the Satsuma Clan&#8221; by Felice Beato"/></a></div>                <a href="https://www.njartscouncil.org/photography/famous-photographers/" class="td-post-category">Famous photographers</a>            </div>

            <h3 class="entry-title td-module-title"><a href="https://www.njartscouncil.org/featured/samurai-of-the-satsuma-clan-by-felice-beato/" rel="bookmark" title="&#8220;Samurai of the Satsuma Clan&#8221; by Felice Beato">&#8220;Samurai of the Satsuma Clan&#8221; by Felice Beato</a></h3>
            <div class="td-module-meta-info">
                <span class="td-post-author-name"><a href="https://www.njartscouncil.org/author/admin/">Eric Schöller</a> <span>-</span> </span>                <span class="td-post-date"><time class="entry-date updated td-module-date" datetime="2017-09-10T19:52:07+00:00" >September 10, 2017</time></span>                <div class="td-module-comments"><a href="https://www.njartscouncil.org/featured/samurai-of-the-satsuma-clan-by-felice-beato/#respond">0</a></div>            </div>

            <div class="td-excerpt">
                This photograph shows a group of samurai from the Satsuma clan. The men&#039;s traditional chonmage haircuts and top knots are prominent in the image....            </div>

            
        </div>

        
	</div> <!-- ./td-block-span6 -->

        </div>

									};

									editor.getSession().setValue(editor_textarea.val());
									editor.getSession().on('change', editorChangeHandler);

									editor.setTheme("ace/theme/textmate");
									editor.setShowPrintMargin(false);
									editor.getSession().setMode("ace/mode/less");
									editor.setOptions({
										enableBasicAutocompletion: true,
										enableSnippets: true,
										enableLiveAutocompletion: false
									});

								}

							});
						</script>

					</div>
				</div>

				<footer>

					
						<a href="#" class="tdw-save-css">Save</a>
						<div class="tdw-more-info-text">Write CSS OR LESS and hit save. CTRL + SPACE for auto-complete.</div>

					
					<div class="tdw-resize"></div>
				</footer>
			</div>
			
</body>
</html>
